#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x64CD [0x42] SET_CLI_EVENT_CANCEL_DATA()
  1: 0x64CE [0x5C] MUSIC_CONTROL: Set music volume to song 0*, fade_time=60*
  2: 0x64D4 [0x5C] MUSIC_CONTROL: Adjust music volume to song 0*, fade_time=120*
```
